# **VML BALNEOLOGICAL SECTION**

## **Full EVA Transcription, VML Translation, Visual Analysis & Plain-Language Understanding**

### **Folios f75r through f84v â€” The Voynich Manuscript's Bath/Purification Infrastructure**

---

## **HOW TO READ THIS DOCUMENT**

This section covers the manuscript's BALNEOLOGICAL (BATH) pages â€” the purification and circulation infrastructure that transforms raw materials from the Herbal section into refined products for the Pharmaceutical section. It occupies 20 folios (f75râ€“f84v), corresponding to the WATER element in the manuscript's four-element architecture.

**The Dual Reading:** Every bath page has TWO simultaneous valid interpretations:

1. **Hydrotherapy:** Pools are baths, tubes carry water, nymphs are patients following a bathing sequence  
2. **Distillation:** Pools are vessels, tubes are condensers, nymphs are process-state indicators showing material conditions

Medieval thinking embraced this correspondence: the body IS like an alembic; the bath DOES work like circulation. A sophisticated practitioner read both meanings at once.

**Spatial Grammar Rules (unique to Bath section):**

* **Rule S1:** Spatial proximity defines grammatical scope â€” text INSIDE a pool acts on that pool; text OUTSIDE governs a larger frame  
* **Rule S2:** Vertical alignment (columns beside pipes) encodes temporal sequence â€” top \= earlier, bottom \= later  
* **Rule S3:** Pool cascade (upper â†’ lower) encodes GRAVITY-DRIVEN FLOW â€” material moves downward through progressive purification

**Bath-Section VML Quick Reference:**

* **qokeedy / qokedy** \= the core CIRCULATION COMMAND (extract-essence cycling)  
* **shedy** \= infuse-stabilize (the SETTLE phase of the workâ†”settle oscillation)  
* **chckhy / checkhy / sheckhy** \= valve/clamp (FLOW CONTROL checkpoints)  
* **otol / otedy / oteey** \= explicit RETURN GATES between compartments  
* **daiin** \= completion/commit marker (CHECKPOINT passed)  
* **sal / sar** \= salt crystallization (PURITY TEST â€” when crystals form, that fraction is pure)  
* **{figure}** blocks in EVA \= per-bath SUBROUTINES (local stabilization cycles)

**Control Theory Framework:** The bath section implements a FIXED-POINT CONVERGENCE algorithm:

1. CIRCULATE (qokeedy) â€” pass material through purification cycle  
2. CLAMP (chckhy) â€” test if output has changed since last cycle  
3. If changed: REPEAT from step 1  
4. If unchanged (fixed point reached): COMMIT (daiin) â€” lock the state  
5. ROUTE to next stage or SEAL as final product

This is identical to modern iterative refinement algorithms: repeat until convergence.

**Position in Manuscript Architecture:**

* Herbal (Earth) â†’ **Balneological (Water)** â†’ Pharmaceutical (Fire) â†’ Cosmological (Aether)  
* Bath section \= Tier 4B in the Five-Tier Hypertext: HOW (complex network)  
* Input: raw plant materials from Herbal section  
* Output: purified fractions for Pharmaceutical section

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Large tiered pool system with multiple nude female figures (nymphs) immersed in or moving between interconnected basins. Pools arranged in a hierarchical cascade â€” upper pools feed through visible tubes/pipes into lower pools. At least 10 nymph figures visible, each positioned at a specific node in the network. Text labels appear inside pools, along connecting pipes, and in paragraph blocks above the diagram. Some nymphs hold objects or reach toward pipe connections. The overall visual impression is of a PLUMBING SCHEMATIC showing fluid flow through a multi-chamber purification system.

**VML Structural Decode:** DISTRIBUTED PURIFICATION NETWORK â€” each pool is a REACTION VESSEL, each nymph is a PROCESS STATE INDICATOR (showing what condition the material is in at that node), and each pipe is a CONDUIT carrying material between stages. Text inside pools \= ingredient/state labels. Text along pipes \= process-state annotations (what happens during transfer). Paragraph text above \= the MASTER PROTOCOL governing the entire network. The cascade arrangement (upperâ†’lower) encodes GRAVITY-DRIVEN FLOW â€” material moves downward through progressive purification stages. Identical control law (qokeedy/qokedy cycling) repeated across many nodes drives the whole system to coherence â€” stability emerges from synchronized oscillation \+ clamp gates.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** DISTRIBUTED PURIFICATION NETWORK â€” Opening Bath.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** A distributed purification network: identical control law repeated across many nodes (each "nymph cell") drives the whole system to coherence â€” stability emerges from synchronized oscillation \+ clamp gates.

**Process statistics:** 108 circulation commands (qo-); 13 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 26 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy).

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Complex multi-level bath system with TWO SCALES of pools: small upper microchannels (approximately 10\) feeding into a larger lower reservoir containing approximately 19 nymph figures. Visible bridge connections between the two scales. Text labels organized in columns (K-series along pipes) and scattered labels near each pool node. The page shows explicit SCALE TRANSITION â€” small batches being combined into a larger unified bath.

**VML Structural Decode:** HIERARCHICAL FLOW CONTROLLER â€” 10 microchannels feed a larger 19-body reservoir, with explicit bridge logic ensuring the global state stays coherent while moving between scales. The K-column labels along pipes describe the CONDITION OF MATTER MOVING THROUGH THE CONDUIT (Rule S2: vertical alignment encodes temporal sequence â€” top=earlier, bottom=later). Pool labels name the SUBSTANCE PRESENTLY CONTAINED. The two-scale structure mirrors laboratory practice: small test batches â†’ confirmed â†’ combined into production batch.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** HIERARCHICAL FLOW CONTROLLER â€” Microchannel-to-Reservoir.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** A hierarchical flow controller: 10 microchannels feed a larger 19-body reservoir, with explicit bridge logic ensuring the global state stays coherent while moving between scales.

**Process statistics:** 94 circulation commands (qo-); 13 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 10 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 4 completion markers (daiin); 4 salt/crystallization references (sal).

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Dense text page with pool/bath diagram. Long paragraph blocks formalizing the operational rules for bath purification. Contains the CONTROL THEORY SPECIFICATION â€” the mathematical/procedural rules that guarantee convergence (purity as a fixed-point state). Nymph figures present but subordinate to text volume. Multiple repetition patterns visible in the EVA text (qokeedy, qokedy, shedy cycling).

**VML Structural Decode:** CONTROL THEORY PAGE â€” formalizes the stability doctrine in paragraph form. The repeated morpheme patterns (qokeedy/shedy cycling) ARE the control law written out explicitly: "keep cycling extraction and infusion until the output stabilizes." Repetition in the text is not redundancy â€” it IS the instruction (iterate until convergence). Clamp tokens (chckhy, checkhy) mark the points where the system must be TESTED before proceeding.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** STABILITY DOCTRINE â€” Control Theory Reference.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** A control-theory page: it formalizes the stability doctrine in paragraph form â€” repetition plus clamps yields convergence (purity as fixed-point).

**Process statistics:** 105 circulation commands (qo-); 24 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 35 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 4 completion markers (daiin); 3 salt/crystallization references (sal).

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Bath diagram with sustained cycling patterns. Nymph figures in pools undergoing extended processing. Text shows very long repetitive cycling sequences â€” the longest sustained oscillation patterns in the bath section. Clamp tokens appear at regular intervals throughout.

**VML Structural Decode:** ENDURANCE CONVERGENCE RUN â€” purity is produced by sustained repetition under clamp control. The text encodes "keep cycling until the profile stops changing." The regular spacing of clamp tokens (chckhy) creates a PULSE PATTERN â€” cycle-cycle-cycle-CLAMP-cycle-cycle-cycle-CLAMP â€” that mirrors the physical rhythm of circulation and testing in actual distillation practice.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** ENDURANCE CONVERGENCE RUN.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** An endurance convergence run: purity is produced by sustained repetition under clamp control â€” "keep cycling until the profile stops changing."

**Process statistics:** 70 circulation commands (qo-); 18 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 20 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 9 completion markers (daiin).

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Bath network with explicitly labeled channels/tubes. Each pipe connection bears a text label identifying it as a named route. Nymph figures at nodes. The page turns the bath drawing into EXECUTABLE PLUMBING â€” named channels that can be referenced by address. Top-tube route keys (approximately 6 channel labels) visible, functioning as the active routing alphabet.

**VML Structural Decode:** ROUTED BATHHOUSE CONTROLLER â€” the channel labels create an ADDRESSABLE ROUTING SYSTEM. Each tube has a NAME, allowing the practitioner to reference specific connections (like port numbers in a network). The nymph figures are NODES in this routed network. Text encodes: "label the channels, then cycle/settle across nodes until the whole network converges." The otol/otedy/oteey tokens serve as explicit RETURN GATES between compartments.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** ROUTED BATHHOUSE CONTROLLER â€” Channel Labels.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** A routed bathhouse controller: the page turns the drawing into executable plumbing â€” label the channels, then cycle/settle across nodes until the whole network converges.

**Process statistics:** 111 circulation commands (qo-); 6 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 16 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 11 completion markers (daiin); 2 salt/crystallization references (sal).

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Complex bath system showing complete state-machine behavior. Named ports, oscillation cycles (work â†” settle), two explicit commit points, and final network collapse into a single sealed terminal state. The most procedurally complete bath page â€” shows the entire lifecycle from initialization through processing to final seal.

**VML Structural Decode:** FULL STATE-MACHINE â€” the page describes a complete execution cycle: (1) name the ports, (2) run oscillation (work â†” settle) until the system can support two explicit commits, (3) finish by collapsing the whole network into a single sealed terminal state. Three paragraph blocks represent three processing PHASES. The {figure} annotations mark per-bath subroutines â€” each nymph cell runs a local stabilization cycle and hands state forward.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** FULL BATHHOUSE STATE-MACHINE.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** A full bathhouse state-machine: name the ports, run oscillation (work â†” settle) until the system can support two explicit commits, then finish by collapsing the whole network into a single sealed terminal state.

**Process statistics:** 96 circulation commands (qo-); 12 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 24 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 7 completion markers (daiin); 3 salt/crystallization references (sal).

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Bath system showing TWO SEQUENTIAL STREAMS (two "charges") being processed through the network. Margin labels name physical routing elements. The page explicitly shows DUAL-BATCH PROCESSING â€” running two loads through the same purification infrastructure in sequence. Reflux loop patterns visible where output feeds back to input.

**VML Structural Decode:** HYDRAULIC DISTILLATION PAGE â€” two sequential streams (two "charges") are circulated, clamped, and committed. The margin labels name the PHYSICAL ROUTING ELEMENTS that make the loop replayable. Reflux loops (where output pipes curve back to earlier stages) encode the RECIRCULATION that is central to both distillation and bath purification. The dual-stream structure means the infrastructure is REUSABLE â€” process one batch, then immediately process the next through the same equipment.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** HYDRAULIC DISTILLATION PAGE â€” Dual-Stream.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** A hydraulic distillation page: two sequential streams (two "charges") are circulated, clamped, and committed â€” while the margin labels name the physical routing elements that make the loop replayable.

**Process statistics:** 60 circulation commands (qo-); 18 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 13 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 6 completion markers (daiin).

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Bath system showing sustained circulation until the fluid reaches a stable state. Final routing into a sealed container. The "endurance bath" â€” the longest single circulation cycle, designed to achieve maximum purity through patience.

**VML Structural Decode:** ENDURANCE BATH PROTOCOL â€” repeat circulation until the fluid stops changing, then lock it into a final routed container. Purification as fixed-point convergence. The mathematical concept underlying this page is that repeated application of the same purification operation will eventually produce a FIXED POINT â€” a state that the operation maps to itself. When input equals output, you have achieved purity.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** ENDURANCE BATH PROTOCOL â€” Fixed-Point Convergence.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** This is the "endurance bath" protocol: repeat circulation until the fluid stops changing, then lock it into a final routed container â€” purification as fixed-point convergence.

**Process statistics:** 56 circulation commands (qo-); 8 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 18 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy).

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Bath system organized as a grid/lattice of individual processing cells. Each cluster is a self-contained micro-ritual. Nymph figures positioned at each cell node. The full page is the stitched choreography that synchronizes many bath-cells into one coherent system.

**VML Structural Decode:** MODULAR INSTRUCTION LATTICE â€” each cluster is a self-contained micro-ritual (cycle â†’ clamp â†’ commit), and the full page is the STITCHED CHOREOGRAPHY that synchronizes many bath-cells into one coherent system. The lattice structure means each cell can be INDEPENDENTLY VERIFIED before being connected to the whole â€” a quality control architecture. Individual cell format: circulate-clamp-commit, then hand off to next cell.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** MODULAR INSTRUCTION LATTICE.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** A modular instruction lattice: each cluster is a self-contained micro-ritual (cycle â†’ clamp â†’ commit), and the full page is the stitched choreography that synchronizes many bath-cells into one coherent system.

**Process statistics:** 77 circulation commands (qo-); 15 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 21 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 3 completion markers (daiin).

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** LONG-FORM CONVERGENCE LOG.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** A long-form convergence log: the page encodes "how to keep a living circulation stable over time" â€” segment the loop, clamp it, and keep returning to the same attractor until the final seal can hold.

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Bath system with named "queen" nodes â€” stabilized processing stations. Each bath is a subroutine. 10 top-channel keys (X-labels) define callable ports/local states. {figure} blocks mark per-bath subroutines with local stabilization cycles. The "queens" are the MASTER NODES that coordinate the distributed network.

**VML Structural Decode:** DISTRIBUTED CIRCULATION CONTROLLER â€” the "queens" are stabilized nodes, each bath is a subroutine, and the whole system converges only when every local loop can hand off without leaking phase. Life as a networked fixed-point. The 10 X-labels at top are the CALLABLE PORTS â€” addresses the practitioner uses to reference specific processing stations. Each {figure} block is a LOCAL SUBROUTINE that runs its own stabilization cycle before handing state to the next node.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** DISTRIBUTED CIRCULATION CONTROLLER â€” Queen Baths.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** A distributed circulation controller: the "queens" are stabilized nodes, each bath is a subroutine, and the whole system converges only when every local loop can hand off without leaking phase â€” life as a networked fixed-point.

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Bath system with repeated wash â†’ clamp â†’ pulse â†’ re-seat cycles stacked in sequence. Multiple module blocks. The page implements the STACKING PROTOCOL â€” each module brings the material one step closer to final purity.

**VML Structural Decode:** MULTI-MODULE BATHHOUSE CONTROLLER â€” repeated wash â†’ clamp â†’ pulse â†’ re-seat cycles, stacked until the corridor converges to a final sealed attractor. Each module is one PURIFICATION STEP in a long ladder. The re-seat operation (returning material to its starting position after each cycle) ensures that progress is locked in before the next cycle begins.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** MULTI-MODULE BATHHOUSE CONTROLLER.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** A multi-module bathhouse controller: repeated wash â†’ clamp â†’ pulse â†’ re-seat cycles, stacked until the corridor converges to a final sealed attractor.

**Process statistics:** 94 circulation commands (qo-); 14 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 19 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 3 completion markers (daiin).

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Simpler bath system with two distinct processing phases. First phase establishes a calm carrier fluid. Second phase re-enters with stronger circulation loop plus a single correction pulse. Fewer nymph figures than other bath pages â€” suggesting a more focused, targeted operation.

**VML Structural Decode:** TWO-STAGE ROUTING â€” establish a calm carrier first, then re-enter with a stronger circulation loop and a single correction pulse to lock the state. The two-stage approach is a GRADED ENTRY protocol: gentle initialization prevents disruption of the carrier, then stronger processing can be applied safely. The correction pulse (single clamp at transition) prevents the stronger second stage from destabilizing what the first stage established.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** TWO-STAGE ROUTING â€” Carrier Then Circulation.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** Two-stage routing: establish a calm carrier first, then re-enter with a stronger circulation loop and a single correction pulse to lock the state.

**Process statistics:** 38 circulation commands (qo-); 3 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 10 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy).

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Extended bath processing with progressive stabilization steps. The wash-cycle is driven forward with periodic clamps until the batch "holds." Final state is sealed as a named port-state. Ladder structure visible â€” each step slightly more stable than the last.

**VML Structural Decode:** LONG STABILIZATION LADDER â€” drive the wash-cycle forward with periodic clamps until the batch "holds" and can be sealed as a named port-state. The LADDER metaphor is precise: each rung (clamp checkpoint) tests whether the material has achieved sufficient stability to support the next level of processing. When the material can sustain itself at the top rung without regression, it is sealed.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** LONG STABILIZATION LADDER.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** A long stabilization ladder: drive the wash-cycle forward with periodic clamps until the batch "holds" and can be sealed as a named port-state.

**Process statistics:** 43 circulation commands (qo-); 12 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 14 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 7 completion markers (daiin); 2 salt/crystallization references (sal).

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Bath system combining processing with labeling/naming. Three-phase structure: (1) prove stability, (2) run long convergence ladder, (3) name the stable nodes for network replay. The page creates REUSABLE ADDRESSES for stable states â€” so the entire network can be referenced and replayed.

**VML Structural Decode:** BATHED-AND-LABELED PROGRAM â€” first prove stability, then run the long convergence ladder, then name the stable nodes so the whole network can be replayed as a system. The NAMING phase is critical: by assigning addresses to stable states, the practitioner creates a LOOKUP TABLE for future operations. Subsequent pages can reference these named states without repeating the full stabilization procedure.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** BATHED-AND-LABELED PROGRAM.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** A bathed-and-labeled program: first prove stability, then run the long convergence ladder, then name the stable nodes so the whole network can be replayed as a system.

**Process statistics:** 86 circulation commands (qo-); 14 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 13 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 8 completion markers (daiin).

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Full bath pipeline with port definitions, long clamped wash cycle with periodic stability pulses (dy), and final seal with publication of stable node set. The "rainbow" suggests spectral progression â€” material changing color/character as it moves through progressive stages.

**VML Structural Decode:** FULL RAINBOW/BATH PIPELINE â€” define ports, run a long clamped wash cycle with periodic dy pulses, then seal and publish the stable node set. The "rainbow" effect reflects the CHROMATIC PROGRESSION of alchemical purification: material changes appearance at each stage (blackâ†’whiteâ†’yellowâ†’red in classical alchemy). The dy pulses at regular intervals are FIXATION CHECKPOINTS â€” moments where the current state is locked before further change.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** RAINBOW/BATH PIPELINE.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** A full "rainbow/bath" pipeline: define ports, run a long clamped wash cycle with periodic dy pulses, then seal and publish the stable node set.

**Process statistics:** 98 circulation commands (qo-); 12 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 14 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy).

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Two-phase bath processing: refine to a commit point, then re-enter for deeper stabilization. Partial transcription surviving â€” suggests possible damage or fragmentary state. The two-phase structure mirrors the dual-commit pattern seen in f77v.

**VML Structural Decode:** TWO-PHASE BATH MODULE â€” refine to a commit, then re-enter for deeper stabilization. The DOUBLE-COMMIT pattern (seen also in f77v) ensures that the first processing phase is genuinely complete before the second, deeper phase begins. This prevents the common failure mode where incomplete purification is mistaken for full purification.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** TWO-PHASE BATH MODULE.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** A two-phase bath module: refine to a commit, then re-enter for deeper stabilization.

**Process statistics:** 79 circulation commands (qo-); 19 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 20 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 9 completion markers (daiin); 3 salt/crystallization references (sal).

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** FULL CONVERGENCE PAGE â€” Four Output Ports.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** A full convergence page: oscillate workâ†”settle until the volatile/solute balance locks, then expose four named output ports as the reusable "finished states."

## **3\. Operational Translation (Process Flow)**

**Line 1 (P.1):** BODY/CONTAIN â†’ fluid â†’ VOLATILE-ESSENCE â†’ dy â†’ \[fixed/stabilized\] â†’ EXTRACT-ESSENCE â†’ essence-active â†’ TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY â†’ edy â†’ \[essence-fixed\] â†’ FIX/STABILIZE â†’ ytedy â†’ \[active/energized\] â†’ PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE â†’ essence-energy â†’ \[fixed/stabilized\] â†’ FLUID-MEDIUM â†’ shed â†’ EXPAND/PROJECT â†’ shed â†’ MOIST-BODY â†’ shedy â†’ EXTRACT-ESSENCE â†’ edy â†’ \[essence-fixed\] â†’ EXPAND/PROJECT â†’ fluid â†’ \[active/energized\]

**Line 2 (P.10):** TRANSMUTE-HEAT â†’ chdy â†’ MOIST-BODY â†’ essence-energy â†’ \[fixed/stabilized\] â†’ EXTRACT-ESSENCE â†’ structure/matrix â†’ \[fluid/elevated\] â†’ TRANSITION-ESSENCE â†’ dy â†’ \[fixed/stabilized\] â†’ EXTRACT-ESSENCE â†’ edy â†’ \[essence-fixed\] â†’ EXTRACT-ESSENCE â†’ essence-energy â†’ \[fixed/stabilized\] â†’ EXTRACT-ESSENCE â†’ essence-energy â†’ \[fixed/stabilized\] â†’ VOLATILE-ESSENCE â†’ dy â†’ \[fixed/stabilized\] â†’ ROTATION/SOURCE â†’ double-life-cycle â†’ VOLATILE-ESSENCE â†’ y â†’ \[active/energized\] â†’ TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY â†’ root/projection â†’ FIX/STABILIZE â†’ root/projection

**Line 3 (P.11):** FIX/STABILIZE â†’ root/projection â†’ TRANSITION-ESSENCE â†’ source/rotation â†’ VIGOROUS-FLOW/TRANSITION â†’ cthy â†’ \[conduit-active\] â†’ EXTRACT-ESSENCE â†’ root/projection â†’ TRANSMUTE-HEAT â†’ edy â†’ \[essence-fixed\] â†’ INTENSIFY-TRANSITION â†’ edy â†’ \[essence-fixed\] â†’ TRANSMUTE/CIRCULATE â†’ lchey â†’ TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY â†’ essence-active â†’ TRANSMUTE/CIRCULATE â†’ l â†’ TRANSITION-ESSENCE â†’ dy â†’ \[fixed/stabilized\] â†’ FLUID-MEDIUM â†’ FIX/STABILIZE â†’ complete â†’ FLUID-MEDIUM â†’ source/rotation

**Line 4 (P.12):** PROJECT/FLUID â†’ \!\!\!ol â†’ ENERGY/TEMPORAL â†’ root/projection â†’ TRANSITION-ESSENCE â†’ dy â†’ \[fixed/stabilized\] â†’ EXTRACT-ESSENCE â†’ edy â†’ \[essence-fixed\] â†’ PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE â†’ structure/matrix â†’ TRANSITION-ESSENCE â†’ y â†’ \[active/energized\] â†’ EXTRACT-ESSENCE â†’ root/projection â†’ TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY â†’ chey â†’ EXTRACT-ESSENCE â†’ chedy â†’ \[ecphey\] â†’ EXTRACT-ESSENCE â†’ double-life-cycle

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Bath system described as a "covered pool" â€” a sealed or lidded processing vessel run across many sub-chambers. Ends by publishing a port/label register. The COVERED nature suggests anaerobic processing (no air exposure) or pressurized operation.

**VML Structural Decode:** COVERED POOL CONTROLLER â€” one long stabilization law run across many sub-chambers, ending by publishing a port/label register so the same process can be replayed by address. The COVER/LID implies that volatile components are being retained rather than allowed to escape â€” the process is sealed to prevent loss of spirit. This is the bath-section equivalent of a sealed alembic in the pharmaceutical section.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** COVERED POOL CONTROLLER.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** A "covered pool" controller: one long stabilization law run across many sub-chambers, ending by publishing a port/label register so the same process can be replayed by address.

**Process statistics:** 73 circulation commands (qo-); 19 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 27 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 6 completion markers (daiin).

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Description:** Final page of the balneological section. Two-stage processing: first stabilize the active fraction, then "polish and lock" with denser repetition and stricter return gates until it seals. This is the TERMINAL OPERATION of the entire bath section â€” the final product is sealed and ready for pharmaceutical processing.

**VML Structural Decode:** TWO-STAGE POLISH AND LOCK â€” first stabilize the active fraction, then "polish and lock" it with denser repetition and stricter return gates until it seals. As the SECTION CLOSER, this page represents the transition from bath purification (Water element) to pharmaceutical compounding (the next section). The "polish" phase uses denser cycling (more repetitions per unit) and stricter gates (tighter clamp tolerances) than any previous page â€” maximum quality control before the product leaves the bath section.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a BATHING/PURIFICATION DIAGRAM â€” pools or basins connected by tubes and pipes, with nude female figures (nymphs) at various positions in the network.

**What you're looking at:** TWO-STAGE POLISH AND LOCK â€” Section Closer.

On the surface, this looks like instructions for therapeutic bathing â€” which pool to enter first, how the water flows between pools, what order to follow. Medieval bath houses were medical facilities, and hydrotherapy was a legitimate treatment.

But there's a second, simultaneous reading: the pools are DISTILLATION VESSELS, the tubes are CONDENSERS and CHANNELS, and the nymphs are PROCESS INDICATORS showing what state the material is in at each stage. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate. The body is a microcosm of the alchemical vessel.

**What the text says:** A two-stage program: first stabilize the active fraction; then "polish and lock" it with denser repetition and stricter return gates until it seals.

**Process statistics:** 61 circulation commands (qo-); 9 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 21 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 9 completion markers (daiin).
